                    </a>
                   </h3>

           </h2>
           <div class="description">

"0px": "/sites/g/files/dprerj316/files/styles/square_sml/public/2019-03/People_moveing_Yellow_stripe_-_iStock-546800756_1300_0.jpg?h=06a766b5&amp;itok=dpVuipjY", "740px": "/sites/g/files/dprerj316/files/styles/wide_med/public/2019-03/People_moveing_Yellow_stripe_-_iStock-546800756_1300_0.jpg?h=5c5b1ce8&amp;itok=VgRZQJ1c", "980px": "/sites/g/files/dprerj316/files/styles/wide_lrg/public/2019-03/People_moveing_Yellow_stripe_-_iStock-546800756_1300_0.jpg?h=5c5b1ce8&amp;itok=KmPZk6Ch"}, "lazy": true, "lazyEdge": "100", "alt": ""}'>
         </div>
         <p class="standout_background_caption">
          Throughout its teaching and research, the School of Public Health trains future public health leaders, advances knowledge on pressing health challenges and enhances population health and well-being.
         </p>
        </div>
        <div class="standout_background_item">
         <div aria-hidden="true" class="js-background standout_background" data-background-options='{"source": {
"0px": "/sites/g/files/dprerj316/files/styles/square_sml/public/2019-03/20170427-sps-emcs-09_1.jpg?h=92f5fc6d&amp;itok=Lvdwm5YB", "740px": "/sites/g/files/dprerj316/files/styles/wide_med/public/2019-03/20170427-sps-emcs-09_1.jpg?h=4b1ab277&amp;itok=9E0c_eN1", "980px": "/sites/g/files/dprerj316/files/styles/wide_lrg/public/2019-03/20170427-sps-emcs-09_1.jpg?h=4b1ab277&amp;itok=aHa4hG24"}, "lazy": true, "lazyEdge": "100", "alt": ""}'>
         </div>
         <p class="standout_background_caption">
          Brown’s School of Professional Studies offers executive education programs designed to advance the careers of accomplished professionals from across the globe.
         </p>
